   <th style="width:15%;">Legal age to smoke any tobacco products </th>

  <tr> 
   <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Flag_of_Algeria.svg/23px-Flag_of_Algeria.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Flag_of_Algeria.svg/35px-Flag_of_Algeria.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Flag_of_Algeria.svg/45px-Flag_of_Algeria.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a> </td> 
   <td align="center">None </td> 
   <td align="center">19 </td> 
   <td>It is illegal to sell tobacco products to minors under the age of 19 years. <br><i>(Chapitre IV sur les problèmes de santé l'article 93: "la vente de tabac ou produits du tabac aux mineurs est interdite".)</i> The legal age to buy tobacco products has been 19 years since June 1984.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> </td>
  </tr>

   <td align="center">None </td>

   <td>It is illegal to sell tobacco to minors under the age of 18.    <td align="center">18 </td> 
   <td>No person shall sell or supply any cigarettes, tobacco or tobacco products to a minor. A person selling or supplying any cigarettes, tobacco or tobacco products to a person who appears to be under 25 years of age shall, before selling or supplying them, ensure, by requiring photo identification, that the latter person is not a minor.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup> </td>

       <td>No vendor or employee of a vendor shall sell or give tobacco or a tobacco product to a person under the age of nineteen years. No person shall purchase tobacco or a tobacco product on behalf of, or for the purpose of resale or give tobacco or a tobacco product, to a person under the age of nineteen years. No person under the age of nineteen years may possess tobacco. </td>

       <td colspan="1" style="text-align:center;">None </td> 
       <td colspan="1" style="text-align:center;">21 (Law exempts individuals born on or before 28 February 2001)<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup> </td> 
       <td>No person shall sell or supply tobacco to a person under the age of 21 years. No person shall purchase or attempt to purchase tobacco on behalf of, or for the purpose of resale to, a person under the age of 21 years. It is legal to supply tobacco to a minor if it is solely for use in traditional Aboriginal spiritual or cultural practices or ceremonies. The minimum legal age for tobacco sales was raised from 19 to 21 on 1 March 2020, after a private members' bill passed third reading on 21 November 2019 and Royal Assent given on 28 November 2019. The bill exempts individuals born on or before 28 February 2001. </td>
      </tr>

The operator of a tobacco retail outlet may not sell tobacco to an adult, if the operator knows the person is purchasing the tobacco for a minor. </td>

       <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Flag_of_Connecticut.svg/20px-Flag_of_Connecticut.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Flag_of_Connecticut.svg/30px-Flag_of_Connecticut.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Flag_of_Connecticut.svg/39px-Flag_of_Connecticut.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="594" data-file-height="459">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Connecticut" title="Connecticut">Connecticut</a> </td>

       <td align="center">21<sup id="cite_ref-wtnh.com_93-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wtnh.com-93">[93]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">[94]</a></sup> </td> 
       <td>Is illegal to sell or give tobacco products to anyone under 21, since 1 October 2019. It is illegal for individuals under 21 to possess tobacco in public.<br><i>A minimum age of 16 was introduced in 1902.</i><br><i>The minimum age was raised from 16 to 18 in 1987 and from 18 to 21 in October 2019.</i> In June 2019, the <a href="/wiki/Connecticut_General_Assembly" title="Connecticut General Assembly">Connecticut General Assembly</a> passed, and the <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Connecticut" class="mw-redirect" title="Governor of Connecticut">Governor of Connecticut</a> signed, a bill into law banning the sale, giving or otherwise distributing tobacco products to anyone under the age of 21 years. Minors under the age of 21 years are explicitly not allowed to attempt to purchase tobacco or to be in the possession of tobacco products. The law took effect on 1 October 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-wtnh.com_93-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wtnh.com-93">[93]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Smoking_and_Health_81-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Smoking_and_Health-81">[81]</a></sup> </td>

Minors under the age of 21 years are explicitly not allowed to attempt to purchase tobacco or to be in the possession of tobacco products. The laws went into effect from 1 August 2019.<br><i>The minimum age of 17 years was introduced in 1953, then increased from 17 to 18 in 1992 and increased again from 18 to 21 in 2019.</i><sup id="cite_ref-fox29.com_95-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-fox29.com-95">[95]</a></sup> </td>

An individual born on or before 1 July 2000 is exempt under state law. However, Portland have stricter regulations and there is no exemptions with regards to the sale and supply of tobacco products to anyone under the age of 21. A person under 21 but born on or before 1 July 2000 may still possess tobacco products legally in the city of Portland. </td>

       <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">21 (Exemption for <a href="/wiki/US_Military" class="mw-redirect" title="US Military">US Military</a> members aged 18-20 and individuals born on or before 31 August 2001)<sup id="cite_ref-easttexasmatters.com_149-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-easttexasmatters.com-149">[149]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">[150]</a></sup> </td> 
       <td>Since 1 September 2019, it is explicitly illegal to sell, give, supply or otherwise provide tobacco to individuals under 21, however <a href="/wiki/US_Military" class="mw-redirect" title="US Military">US Military</a> personnel are exempt.<sup id="cite_ref-easttexasmatters.com_149-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-easttexasmatters.com-149">[149]</a></sup> In addition, anyone born on or before 31 August 2001 is exempt. Minors may not purchase, attempt to purchase, possess, attempt to possess or consume tobacco products in public. Exception: Any individual between 18 and 21 years of age possessing a cigarette or tobacco product in the presence of an adult parent, a guardian, or a spouse of the individual or an employer of the individual, if possession or receipt of the tobacco product is required in the performance of the employee's duties as an employee.<br><i>The minimum age to purchase, possess and consume tobacco was 16 years of age from 1899 to 1989 and 21 years of age since 2019 – however <a href="/wiki/US_Military" class="mw-redirect" title="US Military">US Military</a> personnel are exempt.</i><sup id="cite_ref-easttexasmatters.com_149-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-easttexasmatters.com-149">[149]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-State_ages_'89_–_'94_97-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-State_ages_'89_–_'94-97">[97]</a></sup> </td>

   <td align="center">Varies by state </td> 
   <td align="center">21 </td> 
   <td colspan="4"> <p>As of 2020, federal law required states comply with a minimum age of 21 years for sale/purchase of tobacco products (21 U.S.C. §&nbsp;387f(d)(3)(A)(ii)).<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">[162]</a></sup> State and local laws are permitted to extend this ban and also prohibit supply, possession and consumption to/by persons underage, or increase the age beyond 21. However, most states do not directly ban the consumption of tobacco by a minor. Federal law requiring states to set the minimum age of 21 years is enforced by the Synar Amendment, which requires states to be in compliance with the federal law in order to receive their Substance Abuse Prevention and Treatment Block (SAPTB) grant money (42 U.S.C. 300x-26).<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">[163]</a></sup> In July, the <a href="/wiki/U.S._Department_of_Defense" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Department of Defense">U.S. Department of Defense</a> announced that the purchase age for tobacco on military instillations, including instillations outside the U.S., will be raised to 21 and enforced starting August 1, 2020 in accordance with federal law.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">[164]</a></sup> Before 2020, the federal government had a purchase age of 18. The change went into effect on December 20, 2019, with the passage of the Appropriations for Fiscal Year 2020 signed by President <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">[165]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">[166]</a></sup> </p> </td>
  </tr>

   <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Singapore.svg/23px-Flag_of_Singapore.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Singapore.svg/35px-Flag_of_Singapore.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Singapore.svg/45px-Flag_of_Singapore.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="4320" data-file-height="2880">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Singapore" title="Singapore">Singapore</a> </td> 
   <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">21 </td> 
   <td>Singapore takes a very stern view on underage smoking. The current smoking age in Singapore is 21 years old, after being raised from the previous 18 years old to 19 years old on 1 January 2019 then to 20 on 1 January 2020. It was raised again to 21 on 1 January 2021. <p>It is illegal to sell or give, directly or indirectly any tobacco product to any under-aged person, and anyone caught doing so will be subjected to harsh penalties. </p><p>Anyone caught selling tobacco products to an under-aged person will be charged in court and can be fined up to 5,000 Singapore dollars for the first offense, and up to $10,000 for the second and subsequent offenses. In addition, the store involved will have the tobacco license suspended for 6 months at the first offense, and permanently revoked for the second offense. However, if the store involved is caught selling to minors in school uniform, or to minors below the age of 12, the tobacco license will be permanently revoked even at its first offense. </p><p>Anyone caught buying tobacco products for an under-aged person will be charged in court can be fined up to 2,500 Singapore dollars for the first offence, and up to 5,000 for the second and subsequent offences. </p><p>Anyone caught giving tobacco products to an under-aged person will be charged in court and can be fined up to 500 Singapore dollars for the first offence, and up to 1,000 Singapore dollars for the second and subsequent offences. </p><p>It is illegal for minors to purchase, use or possess any tobacco product in public Minors caught doing so are usually given a warning or a 30-dollar composition fine, with their school and parents informed and follow-up actions taken by the school. Minors caught more than once will have to attend not less than two smoking cessation counseling session to have their offences compounded. Minors who fail to comply with the above requirements or if they are caught four or more times, they can be charged in court and be liable to a fine not exceeding 300 Singapore dollars upon conviction.<sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">[193]</a></sup> </p> </td>
  </tr>

   <td>Minors are not allowed to buy tobacco products.<sup id="cite_ref-244" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-244">[243]</a></sup> </td>
  </tr> 
  <tr> 
   <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Flag_of_Portugal.svg/23px-Flag_of_Portugal.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Flag_of_Portugal.svg/35px-Flag_of_Portugal.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Flag_of_Portugal.svg/45px-Flag_of_Portugal.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="400">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal">Portugal</a> </td> 
   <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">18 </td> 
   <td>It is illegal to sell or give any tobacco product to a minor as well as the consumption of a tobacco product in any public place by a minor. There is a proposition to ban vending machines in places accessible to people younger than 18.<sup id="cite_ref-245" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-245">[244]</a></sup> <br><i>Minimum age was 16 prior to 1 January 2008.</i> </td>
  </tr> 
  <tr> 
   <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Flag_of_Romania.svg/23px-Flag_of_Romania.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Flag_of_Romania.svg/35px-Flag_of_Romania.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Flag_of_Romania.svg/45px-Flag_of_Romania.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="400">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romania</a> </td> 
   <td align="center">None </td> 
   <td align="center">18 </td> 
   <td>There is a ban on sale of tobacco to those younger than 18. Vending machines selling tobacco are banned. There is no minimum legal age of smoking. </td>
  </tr> 
  <tr> 
   <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Russia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Russia.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Russia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Russia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Russia.svg/45px-Flag_of_Russia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> </td> 
   <td align="center">None </td> 
   <td align="center">18 </td> 
   <td>Retail sales of tobacco products to any person under the age of 18 years are an offence.<sup id="cite_ref-246" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-246">[245]</a></sup> </td>
  </tr>

   <td align="center">None </td> 
   <td align="center">18 </td> 
   <td>The sale to persons under 18 is prohibited. Contrary to that, a lot of salesmen sell cigarettes to minors in Serbia. Acquiring tobacco products is very easy for minors despite the law. </td>
  </tr>

   <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;"> <p>18 (purchase de jure) 16 (public possession &amp; purchase de facto) </p> </td> 
   <td><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/23px-Flag_of_England.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/35px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/46px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="480">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a> and <span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Flag_of_Wales_%281959%E2%80%93present%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Wales_%281959%E2%80%93present%29.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Flag_of_Wales_%281959%E2%80%93present%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Wales_%281959%E2%80%93present%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Flag_of_Wales_%281959%E2%80%93present%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_Wales_%281959%E2%80%93present%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="830" data-file-height="498">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Wales" title="Wales">Wales</a>:</b><br>It is illegal to sell tobacco to anyone under the age of 18.<sup id="cite_ref-273" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-273">[272]</a></sup> The minimum age to smoke in public is 16 and authorities have the duty to seize any tobacco or cigarette papers in the possession of any person apparently under the age of 16.<sup id="cite_ref-274" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-274">[273]</a></sup><br><i>Minimum age to purchase was 16 from 1908 to 1 October 2007.</i> <p><i>No minimum age prior to 1908.</i> </p> </td>
  </tr> 
  <tr> 
   <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">18 </td> 
   <td><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Flag_of_Scotland.svg/23px-Flag_of_Scotland.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Flag_of_Scotland.svg/35px-Flag_of_Scotland.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Flag_of_Scotland.svg/46px-Flag_of_Scotland.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a>:</b> <br> A person who sells a tobacco product or cigarette papers to a person under the age of 18 commits an offence. Any person under the age of 18 who buys or attempts to buy a tobacco product or cigarette papers commits an offence as well as an adult who knowlingly buys a tobacco product or cigarette papers on behalf of a person under the age of 18.<sup id="cite_ref-275" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-275">[274]</a></sup> Any constable who has reasonable grounds for suspecting that a person in a public place is under the age of 18, and in possession of a tobacco product or cigarette papers may require the person to surrender the tobacco product.<sup id="cite_ref-276" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-276">[275]</a></sup><br> <p><i>Minimum age was 16 prior to 30 September 2007.</i> </p> </td>
  </tr> 
  <tr> 
   <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">18 </td> 
   <td><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a>:</b><br>A person who sells to a person under the age of 18 any tobacco or cigarette papers, whether for his or her own use or not, shall be guilty of an offence. A member of the <a href="/wiki/Police_Service_of_Northern_Ireland" title="Police Service of Northern Ireland">Police Service of Northern Ireland</a> may seize any tobacco or cigarette papers in the possession of any person apparently under the age of 18 whom he or she finds smoking in any street or public place.<sup id="cite_ref-277" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-277">[276]</a></sup><br> <p><i>Minimum age was 16 prior to 1 September 2008.</i> </p> </td>
  </tr>
